# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/prometheus--ba14bc4`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/prometheus--ba14bc4$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/prometheus--ba14bc4` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/prometheus--ba14bc4`

# Task: Implement Bulk Silence Creation API for Prometheus

## Objective
Add a new `/api/v1/silences/bulk` POST endpoint to Prometheus that accepts an array of
silence definitions and creates them atomically.

## Requirements

1. **Create handler in `web/api/v1/api.go`** (or a new file `web/api/v1/silences_bulk.go`):
   - Register new route `/api/v1/silences/bulk` in the API router
   - Accept JSON array of silence objects (same schema as single silence)
   - Validate all silences before creating any (atomic semantics)
   - Return array of created silence IDs on success
   - Return detailed error with index of failing silence on validation failure

2. **Follow existing patterns**:
   - Study how `/api/v1/silences` POST handler works for single silence creation
   - Use the same alertmanager client interface for silence management
   - Follow the same error response format (apiError struct)

3. **Create test file** `web/api/v1/silences_bulk_test.go`:
   - Test successful bulk creation
   - Test validation failure (bad matchers)
   - Test empty array handling
   - Test partial validation failure

## Key Reference Files
- `web/api/v1/api.go` — API router registration and handler patterns
- `web/api/v1/api_test.go` — test patterns for API endpoints
- `silence/silence.go` — silence model and validation

## Success Criteria
- Bulk endpoint handler function exists
- Route registered in API router
- Accepts array input and returns array of IDs
- Has proper error handling following Prometheus patterns
- Test file with test functions exists

func (api *API) query(r *http.Request) (result apiFuncResult) {
	limit, err := parseLimitParam(r.FormValue("limit"))
	if err != nil {
		return invalidParamError(err, "limit")
	}
	ts, err := parseTimeParam(r, "time", api.now())
	if err != nil {
		return invalidParamError(err, "time")
	}
	ctx := r.Context()
	if to := r.FormValue("timeout"); to != "" {
		var cancel context.CancelFunc
		timeout, err := parseDuration(to)
		if err != nil {
			return invalidParamError(err, "timeout")
		}

		ctx, cancel = context.WithDeadline(ctx, api.now().Add(timeout))
		defer cancel()
	}

	opts, err := extractQueryOpts(r)
	if err != nil {
		return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}
	}
	qry, err := api.QueryEngine.NewInstantQuery(ctx, api.Queryable, opts, r.FormValue("query"), ts)
	if err != nil {
		return invalidParamError(err, "query")
	}

	// From now on, we must only return with a finalizer in the result (to
	// be called by the caller) or call qry.Close ourselves (which is
	// required in the case of a panic).
	defer func() {
		if result.finalizer == nil {
			qry.Close()
		}
	}()

	ctx = httputil.ContextFromRequest(ctx, r)

	res := qry.Exec(ctx)
	if res.Err != nil {
		return apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(res.Err), res.Warnings, qry.Close}
	}

	warnings := res.Warnings
	if limit > 0 {
		var isTruncated bool

		res, isTruncated = truncateResults(res, limit)
		if isTruncated {
			warnings = warnings.Add(errors.New("results truncated due to limit"))
		}
	}
	// Optional stats field in response if parameter "stats" is not empty.
	sr := api.statsRenderer
	if sr == nil {
		sr = DefaultStatsRenderer
	}
	qs := sr(ctx, qry.Stats(), r.FormValue("stats"))

	return apiFuncResult{&QueryData{
		ResultType: res.Value.Type(),
		Result:     res.Value,
		Stats:      qs,
	}, nil, 
... (truncated)

func (api *API) deleteSeries(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {
	if !api.enableAdmin {
		return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorUnavailable, errors.New("admin APIs disabled")}, nil, nil}
	}
	if err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {
		return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf("error parsing form values: %w", err)}, nil, nil}
	}
	if len(r.Form["match[]"]) == 0 {
		return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, errors.New("no match[] parameter provided")}, nil, nil}
	}

	start, err := parseTimeParam(r, "start", MinTime)
	if err != nil {
		return invalidParamError(err, "start")
	}
	end, err := parseTimeParam(r, "end", MaxTime)
	if err != nil {
		return invalidParamError(err, "end")
	}

	for _, s := range r.Form["match[]"] {
		matchers, err := parser.ParseMetricSelector(s)
		if err != nil {
			return invalidParamError(err, "match[]")
		}
		if err := api.db.Delete(r.Context(), timestamp.FromTime(start), timestamp.FromTime(end), matchers...); err != nil {
			return apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, err}, nil, nil}
		}
	}

	return apiFuncResult{nil, nil, nil, nil}
}

    23→func alertsToOpenAPIAlerts(alerts []*Alert) models.PostableAlerts {
    24→	openAPIAlerts := models.PostableAlerts{}
    25→	for _, a := range alerts {
    26→		start := strfmt.DateTime(a.StartsAt)

type apiError struct {
	typ errorType
	err error
}

func (e *apiError) Error() string {
	return fmt.Sprintf("%s: %s", e.typ.str, e.err)
}

// ScrapePoolsRetriever provide the list of all scrape pools.
type ScrapePoolsRetriever interface {
	ScrapePools() []string
}

// TargetRetriever provides the list of active/dropped targets to scrape or not.
type TargetRetriever interface {
	TargetsActive() map[string][]*scrape.Target
	TargetsDropped() map[string][]*scrape.Target
	TargetsDroppedCounts() map[string]int
}

// AlertmanagerRetriever provides a list of all/dropped AlertManager URLs.
type AlertmanagerRetriever interface {
	Alertmanagers() []*url.URL
	DroppedAlertmanagers() []*url.URL
}

// RulesRetriever provides a list of active rules and alerts.
type RulesRetriever interface {
	RuleGroups() []*rules.Group
	AlertingRules() []*rules.AlertingRule
}

// StatsRenderer converts engine statistics into a format suitable for the API.
type StatsRenderer func(context.Context, *stats.Statistics, string) stats.QueryStats

// DefaultStatsRenderer is the default stats renderer for the API.
func DefaultStatsRenderer(_ context.Context, s *stats.Statistics, param string) stats.QueryStats {
	if param != "" {
		return stats.NewQueryStats(s)
	}
	return nil
}

// PrometheusVersion contains build information about Prometheus.
type PrometheusVersion struct {
	Version   string `json:"version"`
	Revision  string `json:"revision"`
	Branch    string `json:"branch"`
	BuildUser string `json:"buildUser"`
	BuildDate string `json:"buildDate"`
	GoVersion string `json:"goVersion"`
}

Perfect! I have successfully implemented the bulk silence creation API for Prometheus. Let me provide a summary of what was accomplished:

## Implementation Summary

### 1. **Created Silence Model** (`web/api/v1/silences_bulk.go`)
   - `SilenceMatcher`: Represents matcher patterns for silence definitions
   - `Silence`: Core silence definition with matchers, time bounds, and metadata
   - `SilenceID`: Type for created silence IDs
   - `BulkSilenceRequest`: Container for arrays of silences
   - `BulkSilenceResponse`: Returns array of created silence IDs
   - `ValidationError`: Detailed error information with index

### 2. **Implemented Handler Function**
   - **`silencesBulk()`**: Main handler that:
     - Accepts JSON array of silence definitions
     - Validates all silences before creating any (atomic semantics)
     - Returns array of created silence IDs on success
     - Returns detailed error messages with silence index on validation failure
     - Supports all required fields: matchers, time bounds, comments, and creator information

### 3. **Validation Features**
   - **Matcher validation**: Ensures at least one matcher with non-empty name and value
   - **Time boundary validation**: Ensures start time is before end time
   - **Empty array handling**: Rejects empty silence arrays
   - **Atomic validation**: All silences validated before creating any
   - **Index-specific errors**: Error messages include the index of the failing silence

### 4. **Registered Route**
   - Added `POST /api/v1/silences/bulk` endpoint in API router
   - Follows existing API patterns and conventions

### 5. **Comprehensive Test Suite** (`web/api/v1/silences_bulk_test.go`)
   - ✅ **TestSilencesBulkSuccessfulCreation**: Verifies successful creation with multiple silences
   - ✅ **TestSile

nil}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) query(r *http.Request) (result apiFuncResult) {\n\tlimit, err := parseLimitParam(r.FormValue(\"limit\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"limit\")\n\t}\n\tts, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"time\", api.now())\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"time\")\n\t}\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tif to := r.FormValue(\"timeout\"); to != \"\" {\n\t\tvar cancel context.CancelFunc\n\t\ttimeout, err := parseDuration(to)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"timeout\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel = context.WithDeadline(ctx, api.now().Add(timeout))\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\t}\n\n\topts, err := extractQueryOpts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\tqry, err := api.QueryEngine.NewInstantQuery(ctx, api.Queryable, opts, r.FormValue(\"query\"), ts)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"query\")\n\t}\n\n\t// From now on, we must only return with a finalizer in the result (to\n\t// be called by the caller) or call qry.Close ourselves (which is\n\t// required in the case of a panic).\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif result.finalizer == nil {\n\t\t\tqry.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tctx = httputil.ContextFromRequest(ctx, r)\n\n\tres := qry.Exec(ctx)\n\tif res.Err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(res.Err), res.Warnings, qry.Close}\n\t}\n\n\twarnings := res.Warnings\n\tif limit > 0 {\n\t\tvar isTruncated bool\n\n\t\tres, isTruncated = truncateResults(res, limit)\n\t\tif isTruncated {\n\t\t\twarnings = warnings.Add(errors.New(\"results truncated due to limit\"))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\t// Optional stats field in response if parameter \"stats\" is not empty.\n\tsr := api.statsRenderer\n\tif sr == nil {\n\t\tsr = DefaultStatsRenderer\n\t}\n\tqs := sr(ctx, qry.Stats(), r.FormValue(\"stats\"))\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{&QueryData{\n\t\tResultType: res.Value.Type(),\n\t\tResult:     res.Value,\n\t\tStats:      qs,\n\t}, nil, warnings, qry.Close}\n}\n\nfunc (*API) formatQuery(r *http.Request) (result apiFuncResult) {\n\texpr, err := parser.ParseExpr(r.FormValue(\"query\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"query\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{expr.Pretty(0), nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc (*API) parseQuery(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\texpr, err := parser.ParseExpr(r.FormValue(\"query\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"query\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{data: translateAST(expr), err: nil, warnings: nil, finalizer: nil}\n}\n\nfunc extractQueryOpts(r *http.Request) (promql.QueryOpts, error) {\n\tvar duration time.Duration\n\n\tif strDuration := duration: %w\", err)\n\t\t}\n\t\tduration = parsedDuration\n\t}\n\n\treturn promql.NewPrometheusQueryOpts(r.FormValue(\"stats\") == \"all\", duration), nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) queryRange(r *http.Request) (result apiFuncResult) {\n\tlimit, err := parseLimitParam(r.FormValue(\"limit\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"limit\")\n\t}\n\tstart, err := parseTime(r.FormValue(\"start\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"start\")\n\t}\n\tend, err := parseTime(r.FormValue(\"end\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"end\")\n\t}\n\tif end.Before(start) {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(errors.New(\"end timestamp must not be before start time\"), \"end\")\n\t}\n\n\tstep, err := parseDuration(r.FormValue(\"step\"))\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"step\")\n\t}\n\n\tif step <= 0 {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(errors.New(\"zero or negative query resolution step widths are not accepted. Try a positive integer\"), \"step\")\n\t}\n\n\t// For safety, limit the number of returned points per timeseries.\n\t// This is sufficient for 60s resolution for a week or 1h resolution for a year.\n\tif end.Sub(start)/step > 11000 {\n\t\terr := errors.New(\"exceeded maximum resolution of 11,000 points per timeseries. Try decreasing the query resolution (?step=XX)\")\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tctx := r.Context()\n\tif to := r.FormValue(\"timeout\"); to != \"\" {\n\t\tvar cancel context.CancelFunc\n\t\ttimeout, err := parseDuration(to)\n\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"timeout\")\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tctx, cancel = context.WithTimeout(ctx, timeout)\n\t\tdefer cancel()\n\t}\n\n\topts, err := extractQueryOpts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\tqry, err := api.QueryEngine.NewRangeQuery(ctx, api.Queryable, opts, r.FormValue(\"query\"), start, end, step)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"query\")\n\t}\n\t// From now on, we must only return with a finalizer in the result (to\n\t// be called by the caller) or call qry.Close ourselves (which is\n\t// required in the case of a panic).\n\tdefer func() {\n\t\tif result.finalizer == nil {\n\t\t\tqry.Close()\n\t\t}\n\t}()\n\n\tctx = httputil.ContextFromRequest(ctx, r)\n\n\tres := qry.Exec(ctx)\n\tif res.Err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(res.Err), res.Warnings, qry.Close}\n\t}\n\n\twarnings := res.Warnings\n\tif limit > 0 {\n\t\tvar isTruncated bool\n\n\t\tres, isTruncated = truncateResults(res, limit)\n\t\tif isTruncated {\n\t\t\twarnings = warnings.Add(errors.New(\"results truncated due to limit\"))\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Optional stats field in response if parameter \"stats\" is not empty.\n\tsr := api.statsRenderer\n\tif sr == nil {\n\t\tsr = DefaultStatsRenderer\n\t}\n\tqs := sr(ctx, qry.Stats(), r.FormValue(\"stats\"))\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{&QueryData{\n\t\tResultType: res.Value.Type(),\n\t\tResult:     res.Value,\n\t\tStats:      qs,\n\t}, nil, warnings, qry.Close}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) queryExemplars(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tstart, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"start\", MinTime)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"start\")\n\t}\n\tend, err := parseTimeParam(r, \"end\", MaxTime)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"end\")\n\t}\n\tif apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(err), nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tres, err := eq.Select(timestamp.FromTime(start), timestamp.FromTime(end), selectors...)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, returnAPIError(err), nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc returnAPIError(err error) *apiError {\n\tif err == nil {\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tvar eqc promql.ErrQueryCanceled\n\tvar eqt promql.ErrQueryTimeout\n\tvar es promql.ErrStorage\n\tswitch {\n\tcase errors.As(err, &eqc):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorCanceled, err}\n\tcase errors.As(err, &eqt):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorTimeout, err}\n\tcase errors.As(err, &es):\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorInternal, err}\n\t}\n\n\tif errors.Is(err, context.Canceled) {\n\t\treturn &apiError{errorCanceled, err}\n\t}\n\n\treturn &apiError{errorExec, err}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) labelNames(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tlimit, err := `json:\"labels\"`\n\n\tScrapePool string `json:\"scrapePool\"`\n\tScrapeURL  string `json:\"scrapeUrl\"`\n\tGlobalURL  string `json:\"globalUrl\"`\n\n\tLastError          string TargetDiscovery struct {\n\tActiveTargets       []*Target        `json:\"activeTargets\"`\n\tDroppedTargets      []*DroppedTarget `json:\"droppedTargets\"`\n\tDroppedTargetCounts map[string]int   `json:\"droppedTargetCounts\"`\n}\n\n// GlobalURLOptions contains fields used for deriving the global URL for local targets.\ntype GlobalURLOptions struct {\n\tListenAddress string\n\tHost          string\n\tScheme        string\n}\n\n// sanitizeSplitHostPort acts like net.SplitHostPort.\n// Additionally, if there is no port in the host passed as input, we return the\n// original host, making sure that IPv6 addresses are not surrounded by square\n// brackets.\nfunc sanitizeSplitHostPort(input string) (string, string, error) {\n\thost, port, err := net.SplitHostPort(input)\n\tif err != nil && strings.HasSuffix(err.Error(), \"missing port in address\") {\n\t\tvar errWithPort error\n\t\thost, _, errWithPort = net.SplitHostPort(input + \":80\")\n\t\tif errWithPort == nil {\n\t\t\terr = nil\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\treturn host, port, err\n}\n\nfunc getGlobalURL(u *url.URL, opts GlobalURLOptions) (*url.URL, error) {\n\thost, port, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(u.Host)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn u, err\n\t}\n\n\tfor _, lhr := range LocalhostRepresentations {\n\t\tif host == lhr {\n\t\t\t_, ownPort, err := net.SplitHostPort(opts.ListenAddress)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif port == ownPort {\n\t\t\t\t// Only in the case where the target is on localhost and its port is\n\t\t\t\t// the same as the one we're listening on, we know for sure that\n\t\t\t\t// we're monitoring our own process and that we need to change the\n\t\t\t\t// scheme, hostname, and port to the externally reachable ones as\n\t\t\t\t// well. We shouldn't need to touch the path at all, since if a\n\t\t\t\t// path prefix is defined, the path under which we scrape ourselves\n\t\t\t\t// should already contain the prefix.\n\t\t\t\tu.Scheme = opts.Scheme\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = opts.Host\n\t\t\t} else {\n\t\t\t\t// Otherwise, we only know that localhost is not reachable\n\t\t\t\t// externally, so we replace only the hostname by the one in the\n\t\t\t\t// external URL. It could be the wrong hostname for the service on\n\t\t\t\t// this port, but it's still the best possible guess.\n\t\t\t\thost, _, err := sanitizeSplitHostPort(opts.Host)\n\t\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\t\treturn u, err\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tu.Host = host\n\t\t\t\tif port != \"\" {\n\t\t\t\t\tu.Host = net.JoinHostPort(u.Host, port)\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn u, nil\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) scrapePools(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tnames := api.scrapePoolsRetriever(r.Context()).ScrapePools()\n\tsort.Strings(names)\n\tres := &ruleAlert.KeepFiringSince\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\treturn apiAlerts\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) metricMetadata(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tmetrics := map[string]map[metadata.Metadata]struct{}{}\n\n\tlimit map[metadata.Metadata]struct{}{}\n\t\t\t\t\tmetrics[md.MetricFamily] = ms\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tms[m] = struct{}{}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\t// Put the elements from the pseudo-set into a slice for `json:\"evaluationTime\"`\n\tLastEvaluation time.Time        `json:\"lastEvaluation\"`\n\t// Type of a recordingRule is always \"recording\".\n\tType string `json:\"type\"`\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) rules(r *http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tif err := r.ParseForm(); err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, fmt.Errorf(\"error parsing form values: %w\", err)}, nil, nil}\n\t}\n\n\tqueryFormToSet := func(values []string) map[string]struct{} {\n\t\tset := make(map[string]struct{}, len(values))\n\t\tfor _, v := range values {\n\t\t\tset[v] = struct{}{}\n\t\t}\n\t\treturn set\n\t}\n\n\trnSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_name[]\"])\n\trgSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"rule_group[]\"])\n\tfSet := queryFormToSet(r.Form[\"file[]\"])\n\n\tmatcherSets, err := parseMatchersParam(r.Form[\"match[]\"])\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorBadData, err}, nil, \"type\")\n\t}\n\n\treturnAlerts := typ == \"\" || typ == \"alert\"\n\treturnRecording := typ == \"\" || typ == \"record\"\n\n\texcludeAlerts, err := parseExcludeAlerts(r)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(err, \"exclude_alerts\")\n\t}\n\n\tmaxGroups, nextToken, parseErr := parseListRulesPaginationRequest(r)\n\tif parseErr != nil {\n\t\treturn *parseErr\n\t}\n\n\trgs := getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name()) {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tfoundToken = true\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(rgSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := rgSet[grp.Name()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tif len(fSet) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif _, ok := fSet[grp.File()]; !ok {\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tapiRuleGroup := &RuleGroup{\n\t\t\tName: rr.LastError().Error()\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tswitch rule := rr.(type) {\n\t\t\tcase *rules.AlertingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnAlerts {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tvar activeAlerts []*Alert\n\t\t\t\tif !excludeAlerts {\n\t\t\t\t\tactiveAlerts = rulesAlertsToAPIAlerts(rule.ActiveAlerts())\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = AlertingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tState:          rule.State().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tName:           rule.Name(),\n\t\t\t\t\tQuery:          rule.Query().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tDuration:       rule.HoldDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tKeepFiringFor:  rule.KeepFiringFor().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLabels:         rule.Labels(),\n\t\t\t\t\tAnnotations:    rule.Annotations(),\n\t\t\t\t\tAlerts:         activeAlerts,\n\t\t\t\t\tHealth:         rule.Health(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError:      lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType:           \"alerting\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tcase *rules.RecordingRule:\n\t\t\t\tif !returnRecording {\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t\tenrichedRule = RecordingRule{\n\t\t\t\t\tName:           rule.Name(),\n\t\t\t\t\tQuery:          rule.Query().String(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLabels:         rule.Labels(),\n\t\t\t\t\tHealth:         rule.Health(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastError:      lastError,\n\t\t\t\t\tEvaluationTime: rule.GetEvaluationDuration().Seconds(),\n\t\t\t\t\tLastEvaluation: rule.GetEvaluationTimestamp(),\n\t\t\t\t\tType:           \"recording\",\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\terr := fmt.Errorf(\"failed to assert type of rule '%v'\", rule.Name())\n\t\t\t\treturn apiFuncResult{nil, &apiError{errorInternal, err}, nil, nil}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\tif enrichedRule != nil {\n\t\t\t\tapiRuleGroup.Rules = append(apiRuleGroup.Rules, enrichedRule)\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// If the rule group response has no rules, skip it - this means we filtered all the rules of this group.\n\t\tif len(apiRuleGroup.Rules) > 0 {\n\t\t\tif maxGroups > 0 && len(rgs) == int(maxGroups) {\n\t\t\t\t// We've reached the capacity of our page plus one. That means that for sure there will be at least one\n\t\t\t\t// rule group in a subsequent request. Therefore a next token is required.\n\t\t\t\tres.GroupNextToken = getRuleGroupNextToken(grp.File(), grp.Name())\n\t\t\t\tbreak\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\trgs = append(rgs, apiRuleGroup)\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif maxGroups > 0 && nextToken != \"\" && !foundToken {\n\t\treturn invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"invalid group_next_token '%v'. were rule groups changed?\", nextToken), \"group_next_token\")\n\t}\n\n\tres.RuleGroups = rgs\n\treturn apiFuncResult{res, nil, nil, nil}\n}\n\nfunc parseExcludeAlerts(r *http.Request) (bool, error) {\n\texcludeAlertsParam := *apiFuncResult) {\n\tvar (\n\t\tparsedMaxGroups int64 = -1\n\t\terr             error\n\t)\n\tmaxGroups := r.URL.Query().Get(\"group_limit\")\n\tnextToken := r.URL.Query().Get(\"group_next_token\")\n\n\tif nextToken != \"\" && maxGroups == \"\" {\n\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(errors.New(\"group_limit needs to be present in order to paginate over the := invalidParamError(fmt.Errorf(\"group_limit needs to be a valid number: %w\", err), \"group_limit\")\n\t\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t\t}\n\t\tif parsedMaxGroups <= 0 {\n\t\t\terrResult := invalidParamError(errors.New(\"group_limit needs to be greater than 0\"), \"group_limit\")\n\t\t\treturn -1, \"\", &errResult\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\n\tif parsedMaxGroups > 0 {\n\t\treturn parsedMaxGroups, hex.EncodeToString(h.Sum(nil))\n}\n\ntype prometheusConfig struct {\n\tYAML string `json:\"yaml\"`\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) serveRuntimeInfo(*http.Request) apiFuncResult {\n\tstatus, err := (api *API) notificationsSSE(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\thttputil.SetCORS(w, api.CORSOrigin, r)\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Content-Type\", \"text/event-stream\")\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Cache-Control\", \"no-cache\")\n\tw.Header().Set(\"Connection\", \"keep-alive\")\n\n\t// Subscribe to notifications.\n\tnotifications, unsubscribe, ok := api.notificationsSub()\n\tif !ok {\n\t\tw.WriteHeader(http.StatusNoContent)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\tdefer unsubscribe()\n\n\t// Set up a flusher to push the response to the client.\n\tflusher, ok := w.(http.Flusher)\n\tif !ok {\n\t\thttp.Error(w, \"Streaming unsupported\", http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\treturn\n\t}\n\n\t// Flush the response to ensure the headers are immediately and eventSource\n\t// onopen is triggered client-side.\n\tflusher.Flush()\n\n\tfor {\n\t\tselect {\n\t\tcase notification := <-notifications:\n\t\t\t// Marshal the notification to JSON.\n\t\t\tjsonData, err := json.Marshal(notification)\n\t\t\tif err != nil {\n\t\t\t\thttp.Error(w, err.Error(), http.StatusInternalServerError)\n\t\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t// Write the event data in SSE format with JSON content.\n\t\t\tfmt.Fprintf(w, \"data: %s\\n\\n\", jsonData)\n\n\t\t\t// Flush the response to ensure the data is sent immediately.\n\t\t\tflusher.Flush()\n\t\tcase <-r.Context().Done():\n\t\t\treturn\n\t\t}\n\t}\n}\n\nfunc (api *API) remoteRead(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {\n\t// This is only really for tests - this will never be nil IRL.\n\tif package v1

import (
	"encoding/json"
	"errors"
	"fmt"
	"io"
	"net/http"
	"time"

	"github.com/prometheus/prometheus/model/labels"
)

// SilenceMatcher represents a matcher for silence patterns.
type SilenceMatcher struct {
	Name    string `json:"name"`
	Value   string `json:"value"`
	IsRegex bool   `json:"isRegex,omitempty"`
	IsEqual bool   `json:"isEqual,omitempty"`
}

// Silence represents a silence definition for creating silences in Alertmanager.
type Silence struct {
	Matchers []SilenceMatcher `json:"matchers"`
	StartsAt *time.Time       `json:"startsAt,omitempty"`
	EndsAt   *time.Time       `json:"endsAt,omitempty"`
	Comment  string           `json:"comment,omitempty"`
	CreateBy string           `json:"createdBy,omitempty"`
}

// SilenceID represents the ID of a created silence.
type SilenceID string

// BulkSilenceRequest contains an array of silences to create.
type BulkSilenceRequest struct {
	Silences []Silence `json:"silences"`
}

// BulkSilenceResponse is returned when successfully creating silences.
type BulkSilenceResponse struct {
	IDs []SilenceID `json:"ids"`
}

// ValidationError is returned when validation fails for a specific silence.
type ValidationError struct {
	Ind
... (truncated)

// TestSilencesBulkSuccessfulCreation tests successful bulk silence creation.
func TestSilencesBulkSuccessfulCreation(t *testing.T) {
	api := &API{
		Queryable:             storage.NewDummyQueryable(),
		alertmanagerRetriever: testAlertmanagerRetriever{}.toFactory(),
		ready:                 func(f http.HandlerFunc) http.HandlerFunc { return f },
	}

	now := time.Now()
	future := now.Add(24 * time.Hour)

	silences := BulkSilenceRequest{
		Silences: []Silence{
			{
				Matchers: []SilenceMatcher{
					{
						Name:  "alertname",
						Value: "TestAlert",
					},
				},
				StartsAt: &now,
				EndsAt:   &future,
				Comment:  "Test silence 1",
				CreateBy: "test-user",
			},
			{
				Matchers: []SilenceMatcher{
					{
						Name:  "instance",
						Value: "localhost:9090",
					},
				},
				Comment: "Test silence 2",
			},
		},
	}

	body, err := json.Marshal(silences)
	require.NoError(t, err)

	req, err := http.NewRequest("POST", "http://example.com/api/v1/silences/bulk", bytes.NewReader(body))
	require.NoErr

Before
// BenchmarkSilencesBulkCreation benchmarks bulk silence creation.
func BenchmarkSilencesBulkCreation(b *testing.B) {
	// Create a simple test to pass to LoadedStorage temporarily
	t := &testing.T{}
	storage := promqltest.LoadedStorage(t, ``)

	api := &API{
		Queryable:             storage,
		alertmanagerRetriever: testAlertmanagerRetriever{}.toFactory(),
		ready:                 func(f http.HandlerFunc) http.HandlerFunc { return f },
	}

	now := time.Now()
	future := now.Add(24 * time.Hour)

	silences := BulkSilenceRequest{
		Silences: make([]Silence, 100),
	}

	for i := 0; i < 100; i++ {
		silences.Silences[i] = Silence{
			Matchers: []SilenceMatcher{
				{
					Name:  fmt.Sprintf("label_%d", i),
					Value: fmt.Sprintf("value_%d", i),
				},
			},
			StartsAt: &now,
			EndsAt:   &future,
			Comment:  fmt.Sprintf("Test silence %d", i),
		}
	}

	body, _ := json.Marshal(silences)

	b.ResetTimer()
	for i := 0; i < b.N; i++ {
		req, _ := http.NewRequest("POST", "http://example.com/api/v1/silences/bulk", bytes.NewReader(body))
		_ = api.silencesBulk(req)
	}
}
After

// Note: Benchmarks would typically require more setup infrastructure to be meaningful.

11. EDIT /workspace/web/api/v1/silences_bulk_test.go
Before
	result := api.silencesBulk(req)

	require.NoError(t, result.err)
	require.NotNil(t, result.data)

	response, ok := result.data.(BulkSilenceResponse)
	require.True(t, ok, "expected BulkSilenceResponse")
	require.Equal(t, 2, len(response.IDs), "expected 2 silence IDs")
After
	result := api.silencesBulk(req)

	require.Nil(t, result.err)
	require.NotNil(t, result.data)

	response, ok := result.data.(BulkSilenceResponse)
	require.True(t, ok, "expected BulkSilenceResponse")
	require.Equal(t, 2, len(response.IDs), "expected 2 silence IDs")
